\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NanoSVG\ is\ a\ simple\ stupid\ single-\/header-\/file\ SVG\ parse.\ The\ output\ of\ the\ parser\ is\ a\ list\ of\ cubic\ bezier\ shapes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ library\ suits\ well\ for\ anything\ from\ rendering\ scalable\ icons\ in\ your\ editor\ application\ to\ prototyping\ a\ game.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NanoSVG\ supports\ a\ wide\ range\ of\ SVG\ features,\ but\ something\ may\ be\ missing,\ feel\ free\ to\ create\ a\ pull\ request!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ shapes\ in\ the\ SVG\ images\ are\ transformed\ by\ the\ viewBox\ and\ converted\ to\ specified\ units.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ That\ is,\ you\ should\ get\ the\ same\ looking\ data\ as\ your\ designed\ in\ your\ favorite\ app.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NanoSVG\ can\ return\ the\ paths\ in\ few\ different\ units.\ For\ example\ if\ you\ want\ to\ render\ an\ image,\ you\ may\ choose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ get\ the\ paths\ in\ pixels,\ or\ if\ you\ are\ feeding\ the\ data\ into\ a\ CNC-\/cutter,\ you\ may\ want\ to\ use\ millimeters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ units\ passed\ to\ NanoSVG\ should\ be\ one\ of:\ 'px',\ 'pt',\ 'pc'\ 'mm',\ 'cm',\ or\ 'in'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ DPI\ (dots-\/per-\/inch)\ controls\ how\ the\ unit\ conversion\ is\ done.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ you\ don't\ know\ or\ care\ about\ the\ units\ stuff,\ "{}px"{}\ and\ 96\ should\ get\ you\ going.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Example\ Usage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ //\ Load\ SVG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ NSVGimage*\ image;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ image\ =\ nsvgParseFromFile("{}test.svg"{},\ "{}px"{},\ 96);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ printf("{}size:\ \%f\ x\ \%f\(\backslash\)n"{},\ image-\/>width,\ image-\/>height);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ //\ Use...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ for\ (NSVGshape\ *shape\ =\ image-\/>shapes;\ shape\ !=\ NULL;\ shape\ =\ shape-\/>next)\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ (NSVGpath\ *path\ =\ shape-\/>paths;\ path\ !=\ NULL;\ path\ =\ path-\/>next)\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ (int\ i\ =\ 0;\ i\ <\ path-\/>npts-\/1;\ i\ +=\ 3)\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ float*\ p\ =\ \&path-\/>pts[i*2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ drawCubicBez(p[0],p[1],\ p[2],p[3],\ p[4],p[5],\ p[6],p[7]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ //\ Delete}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ nsvgDelete(image);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
